SBYIN PA PO

BSOD SNYOMS PA CHUNG NGU GANG ZHE NA, GANG ZHIG LAG PA GNYIS KYIS
BCAD NAS BZA' BAR NUS PA STE, 'DI NI LHUNG BZED KYI BSOD SNYOMS
PA CHUNG NGU'O, ,LHUNG BZED KYI BSOD SNYOMS PA 'BRING NYID GANG
ZHE NA, GANG ZHIG LAG PA

GCIG GIS BCAD NAS ZA BAR NUS PA STE, 'DI NI LHUNG BZED KYI BSOD
SNYOMS PA 'BRING DU 'DOD DO, ,LHUNG BZED KYI BSOD SNYOMS PA CHEN
PO GANG ZHE NA, LAG PA GCIG GIS BCAD NAS MA YIN, KHAS BCAD NAS MA
YIN, 'JIG PAR MI BYED 'JIG TU 'JUG PAR MI BYED CING, GANG

BSHIG NAS RNYED PA ZA BA STE, 'DI NI LHUNG BZED KYI BSOD SNYOMS
PA CHEN PO'O, ,CI ZHIG BKAG PA LAS SBYANGS PA'I YAN LAG MTHAR
GYIS SLONG BA'I BSOD SNYOMS PA YANG DAG PAR LEN PA YIN ZHE NA,
BSHAD PA, MTHON PO'I KHYIM DGAG PA'I PHYIR SBYANGS PA'I YAN LAG
MTHAR GYIS SLONG BA'I

BSOD SNYOMS PA YANG DAG PAR LEN PA YIN NO, ,DE LA MTHAR GYIS
SLONG BA'I BSOD SNYOMS PA NI RNAM PA GSUM STE, CHUNG NGU DANG
'BRING DANG CHEN PO'O, ,MTHAR GYIS SLONG BA'I BSOD SNYOMS PA
CHUNG NGU GANG ZHE NA, GANG ZHIG GRONG DU BSOD SNYOMS LA PHYIN PA
NA KUN DGA' BAR GNAS PAS RNYED PA STE, 'DI

NI MTHAR GYIS SLONG BA'I BSOD SNYOMS PA CHUNG NGU'O, ,MTHAR GYIS
SLONG BA'I BSOD SNYOMS PA 'BRING NYID GANG ZHE NA, BSOD SNYOMS PA
'GRO BA NA KUN DGA' RA BAN GNAS PAS MI LEN CING BAR GYI LAM DU
RNYED PA LEN PA STE, 'DI NI MTHAR GYIS SLONG BA'I BSOD SNYOMS PA
'BRING NYID DO, ,MTHAR GYIS

YANG BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA' SBYIN PAR BYA BA'I CHOS DAG YOD DE BDOG

PO 'DI NI MDOR BSDU NA, BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I THAMS CAD KYI SGO
NAS SBYIN PA ZHES BYA'O, ,DE LA BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I SKYES BU
DAM PA RNAMS KYI SKYES BU DAM PA'I SBYIN PA GANG ZHE NA, BYANG
CHUB SEMS DPA' NI DAD PA DANG, BKUR STI DANG,

RANG GI LAG DAR BA DANG, DUS LA BAB PA DANG GZHAN LA MI GNAD PAR
SBYIN PA SBYIN PAR BYED PA GANG YIN PA 'DI NI, BYANG CHUB SEMS
DPA'I SKYES BU DAM PA RNAMS KYI SKYES BU DAM PA'I SBYIN PA ZHES
BYA'O, ,DE LA BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I RNAM PA THAMS CAD KYI SBYIN
PA GANG ZHE NA, MI BRTEN PAR SBYIN

@185B PA DANG, MI SRI BAR SBYIN PA DANG, DGA' BAS SBYIN PA DANG,
RGYUN MI 'CHAD PAR SBYIN PA DANG, SNOD LA SBYIN PA DANG, SNOD MA
YIN PA LA SBYIN PA DANG, THAMS CAD SBYIN PA DANG, KUN LA SBYIN PA
DANG, DUS THAMS CAD DU SBYIN PA DANG, KHA NA MA THO BA MED PA'I
SBYIN PA DANG, SEMS CAN GYI DNGOS PO

THAMS CAD SBYIN PA DANG, YUL GYI DNGOS PO SBYIN PA DANG, NOR DANG
'BRU'I DNGOS PO SBYIN PA DANG, SBYIN PA RNAM PA BCU GSUM PO NI
BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I RNAM PA THAMS CAD KYI SBYIN PA ZHES BYA'O,
,DE LA BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I PHONGS SHING 'DOD PA LA SBYIN PA
GANG ZHE NA, 'DI LA BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'

ZAS DANG SKOM GYIS PHONGS SHING 'DOD PA RNAMS LA NI ZAS DANG SKOM
SBYIN PAR BYED PA DANG, BZHON PA 'DOD PA RNAMS LA NI BZHON PA
DANG, GOS 'DOD PA RNAMS LA NI GOS DANG, RGYAN 'DOD PA RNAMS LA NI
RGYAN DANG, SNOD SPYAD RNAM PA SNA TSOGS 'DOD PA RNAMS LA NI SNOD
SPYAD RNAM PA SNA TSOGS SBYIN PAR

BYED PA DANG, SPOS DANG, ME TOG DANG, PHRENG BA DANG, BYUG PA
'DOD PA RNAMS LA SPOS DANG, ME TOG DANG, PHRENG BA DANG, BYUG PA
DANG, GNAS 'DOD PA RNAMS LA NI GNAS DANG, SNANG BAS PHONGS SHING
'DOD PA RNAMS LA NI SNANG BA SBYIN PAR BYED PA DANG, RNAM PA
BRGYAD PO 'DI DAG NI BYANG CHUB

SEMS DPA'I PHONGS SHING 'DOD PA LA SBYIN PA YIN PAR RIG PAR
BYA'O, ,DE LA BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I TSE 'DI DANG GZHAN DU BDE BAR
'GYUR BA'I SBYIN PA GANG ZHE NA, ZANG ZING GI SBYIN PA DANG, CHOS
KYI SBYIN PA DANG, MI 'JIGS PA SBYIN PA'I SBYIN PA NI MDOR BSDU
NA SEMS CAN RNAMS KYI 'DI DANG GZHAN

DU BDE BAR 'GYUR BA'I SBYIN PA YIN PAR RIG PAR BYA'O, ,ZANG ZING
GI SBYIN PA DE NI SER SNA'I DRI MA DANG, GSOG 'JOG GI DRI MA BSAL
NAS, BZANG PO DANG, GTZANG MA DANG, RUNG BA SBYIN PAR BYED PA'O,
,DE LA SER SNA'I DRI MA BSAL BA NI SEMS KYIS KUN DU 'DZIN PA
YONGS SU GTANG BA'I PHYIR RO, ,GSOG

GE DANG, STAG DANG, CHU SRIN 'DZIN KHRI DANG, RGYAL PO DANG, CHOM
RKUN DANG, CHU LA SOGS PA'I 'JIGS PA LAS YONGS SU SKYOB PA YIN
PAR RIG PAR BYA'O,,

PA'I SBYIN PA GANG ZHE NA,

DANG, MU GE'I DUS NA SBYIN BDAG TU 'GYUR BA DANG, SLONG BA PO
RNAMS NYE BAR DONG BA NA 'DI'I KHYIM MA BSGRIBS PAR 'GYUR BA
DANG, STER BA'AM LEN PA NA 'DI LA 'GA' YANG PHRAG DOG PAR MI
'GYUR BA STE, SH'A RI'I BU 'DI DAG NI BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'

PHRAG DOG DANG SER SNA YONGS SU SPANGS PA'I PHAN YON BZHI YIN NO
ZHES GSUNGS SO, ,LAS RAB TU RNAM PAR 'BYED PA'I MDO LAS KYANG, DE
LA ZAS BYIN PA NA CHOS BCU 'PHEL BAR 'GYUR BA GANG ZHE NA, BZA'
BA BYIN PA NA KHA DOG DANG LDAN PAR 'GYUR BA DANG STOBS DANG LDAN
PAR 'GYUR BA DANG, SKYID PAR

'GYUR BA DANG, SPOBS PA DANG LDAN PAR 'GYUR BA DANG, TSE RING
ZHING YUN RING DU 'TSO BAR 'GYUR BA DANG, BZA' BA DANG BTUNG BA
MANG BAR 'GYUR BA DANG, RIGS MTHO BAR 'GYUR BA DANG, LONGS SPYOD
CHE BAR 'GYUR BA DANG, MTHO RIS SU SKYE BAR 'GYUR BA DANG, MYUR
DU MYA NGAN LAS 'DA' BAR 'GYUR TE, BZA' BA

BYIN PA NA CHOS BCU PO 'DI DAG 'PHEL BAR 'GYUR RO ZHES GSUNGS SO,
,RAB TU BYUNG BAR GTOGS PA'I SBYIN PA DANG, KHYIM LA SER SNA BYED
PA DANG, TSUL 'CHOS PA DANG, LOG PAR 'TSO BA DANG, CHOS SMRA BA
LA SKUR PA 'DEBS PA DANG, CHOS SPONG BA DANG, RMA 'BYIN PA DANG,
ZHAL TA BYED PA DANG, YONGS

@198A *, ,SU 'DZIN PA DANG, 'TSO BA YANG BA DANG, 'TSO BA YONGS
SU DAG PA DANG, RNYED PA DANG BKUR STI DANG, BDUD KYIS SMRAS PA
DANG, NYO TSONG DANG, TSUL KHRIMS 'CHAL PA'I MTSAN MA DANG,
TSUL KHRIMS DANG LDAN PA ZIL GYIS GNON PA DANG, RAB TU BYUNG BA
LA BSNGAGS PA DANG, SBYANGS PA'I YON TAN DANG, SPYOD YUL MA

YIN PA DANG, SDIG PA'I GROGS PO DANG, DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN DANG,
DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA LA MCHOD PA DANG RIM GRO BYA BA DANG, DAM PA'I
CHOS YONGS SU 'DZIN PA DANG, DAM PA'I CHOS NUB PAR 'GYUR BA DANG,
THOS PA'I YON TAN BRJOD PA DANG, THOS PA NYUNG BA SPANG BA DANG,
MI 'DRI BA'I SKYON DANG, CHOS RKU BA DANG, BDAG LA

BSTOD CING GZHAN LA SMOD PA DANG, BYANG CHUB KYI SEMS KYI YON TAN
BRJOD PA DANG, BYANG CHUB KYI SEMS LA 'DUN PA BZLOG PA DANG,
BYANG CHUB KYI SEMS BRJED PA DANG, GSO DPYAD DGAG PA DANG, RGYU
SKAR BRTAG PA SPANG BA DANG, RGYAL PO LA BRTEN PA SMAD PA DANG,
KHYIM PA'I SBYIN PA DANG, SBYIN PA'I MI MTHUN PA'I PHYOGS DANG,

SBYIN PA'I YON TAN LA DGONGS PA BSTAN PA'O, ,MDO SDE SNA TSOGS
LAS BTUS PA'I GTAM RDZOGS SO,, ,,SBYIN PAR BYA BA'I CHOS 'DI NI
RAB MCHOG THEG PA CHEN PO'I RJES SU 'BRANG BA SH'A KYA'I GNAS
BRTAN MKHAS BA CHEN PO DPAL MAR ME MDZAD YE SHES KYI YIN NO,
,GANG 'DIR BSOD NAMS SU GYUR PA DE MKHAN PO DANG SLOB

DPON DANG PHA DANG MA SNGON DU 'GRO BAR BYAS TE, SEMS CAN GYI
TSOGS MTHA' DAG BLA NA MED PA'I YE SHES KYI 'BRAS BU THOB PAR BYA
BA'I CHED DU GYUR CIG ,THUB PA'I GSUNG RAB RGYA MTSO'I BDUD
RTZI'I BCUD, ,LTUNG DANG NYON MONGS NAD GSO'I SMAN CHEN 'DI,
,LNGA BRGYA'I DUS NA BSTAN PA'I SROG 'DZIN PA, ,SH'A KYA'I SRAS

PO YON TAN GRAGS PA YIS, ,DPE MED GRONG DU SKU 'KHRUNGS RTZOD DUS
KYI, ,MKHAS PA RGYAL BA KUN DGA' LA GSOL NAS, ,YA RABS SPYOD PA
MA NYAMS DAD DANG LDAN, ,PA TSA BA LDONG GI SA SKOR ZHOGS KYI
STONG, MKHAS BTZUN 'BYUNG GNAS DAM PAS BYIN BRLABS PA, ,DPAL
LDAN YA GAD GTZUG LAG KHANG CHEN DU, ,

SKAD GNYIS SMRA LA SENG GE'I SGRA SGROGS PA, ,SH'A KYA'I DGE
SLONG NYI MA GRAGS PA DANG, ,KHU YI PHAN [?] DE MDO SDE 'BAR GYIS
BSGYUR, ,DES BSKYED BSOD NAMS ZLA LTAR BSIL BA YIS, ,THUB PA'I
'KHOR BZHI DANG NI 'GRO KUN GYI, ,LTUNG DANG NYON MONGS GDUNG BA
